Im Gegensatz zur amerikanischen, britischen, und kanadischen Notenbank hat die Europäische Zentralbank (EZB) den Leitzsins nicht gesenkt. Ihrem Ermessen nach würden die Zinssenkung die steigenden Rohstoffpreise und der leichte Rückgang der Arbeitslosigkeit die Entstehung einer Inflationsspirale begünstigen.	As opposed to the US, UK, and Canadian central banks, the European Central Bank (ECB) did not cut interest rates, arguing that a rate drop combined with rising raw material prices and declining unemployment would trigger an inflationary spiral.	Unlike the US, British and Canadian Federal Reserve, the European Central Bank (ECB) has not lowered the key rate and it is their opinion that interest rate reductions would encourage rising commodity prices and a slight reduction in unemployment to lead to inflation spiralling.

Political Capital: Ungarische Garde erhöht Staatsrisiko	Political Capital: The Hungarian Guard has heightened the country's risk level	Political Capital: Hungarian Guard increases state risk
Nach Ansicht der Abteilung für Risikoanalyse (Risk Analysing Division) von Political Capital haben die Aktivitäten der in diesem August mit Unterstützung der "Bewegung für ein besseres Ungarn" gegründeten Ungarischen Garde das Risiko Ungarns und der Region in mehrerer Hinsicht angehoben.	Actions by the Hungarian Guard, established in August with the support of the Movement for a Righter Hungary, has raised the political risk level of Hungary and the entire region from a number of aspects, according to the Risk Analysing Division of Political Capital.	The Risk Analysis Division department of political Capital believes that the activities of the Hungarian Guard, founded this August with the support of the 'Movement for a Better Hungary', have increased the risk of Hungary and the region in several respects.
Im "Risikowarnungs-Bericht" des Instituts heißt es unter anderem: Im Zusammenhang mit den Aktivitäten der Ungarischen Garde stellt das höchste politische Risiko die "Verschärfung der bereits bestehenden ethnischen Spannungen zwischen der Zigeuner und Nicht-Zigeunerbevölkerung in Ungarn dar, die sogar kurzfristig zu gewalttätigen ethnischen Auseinandersetzungen führen könnte".	The research entity issued a "risk warning," writing: the actions of the Hungarian Guard are triggering an exceeding political risk "that the already existing ethnic tensions between the Gypsy and non-Gypsy residents of Hungary could heat up to toxic levels as early as the short-term, leading to ethnic conflicts that could turn violent."	The Institute's Risk Alert Report states, among other things, that, in the context of the activities of the Hungarian Guard, the greatest political risk is' exacerbating the already existing ethnic tensions between the Gypsies and non-Gypsies in Hungary, which could even lead to violent ethnic clashes in the short term '.
Hauptgrund dafür sei die Strategie der Ungarischen Garde, die vermutlich auf die Provokation einer solchen Auseinandersetzung abzielt, so das Forschungsinstitut.	The major reason for this is that Hungarian Guard's political strategy appears to be aimed at provoking action of this nature, the research institute added.	The main reason for this is the strategy of the Hungarian Guard, which is probably intended to provoke such a dispute, according to the research institute.
Wie berichtet, wird dies als Versäumnis von Seiten der politisch Verantwortlichen angesehen: "Personen des öffentlichen Lebens haben die Diskussion der Roma-Frage Vertretern radikaler politischer Gruppierungen überlassen, die nun ihre politische Strategie auf den Roma-Ungarn-Gegensatz aufgebaut haben".	This is the outcome of one of the most serious failures of Hungary's political players: "The primary actors in public life turned over public debate of Roma issues to representatives of the radical and extremist political forces, who have built a political strategy out of Gypsy-Hungarian differences."	As is reported, this is seen as a failure on the part of political leaders: 'Public figures have left discussion of the Roma issue to representatives of radical political groups, who have now built their political strategy on the Roma Hungarian opposition'.
Man vermutet, dass dies das Problem verschärfen, den vernünftigen Dialog unmöglich machen, Extremitäten begünstigen, sowie die Wahrscheinlichkeit gewalttätiger Auseinandersetzungen erhöhen würde.	This, Political Capital believes, has intensified the problem, rendering any normal dialogue impossible, reinforcing the extremists, and heightening the probability that violent conflicts will occur.	It is suspected that this would exacerbate the problem, make it impossible to have a proper dialogue, foster extremes and increase the likelihood of violent clashes.
Das Forschungsinstitut meint außerdem, die Tätigkeiten der Ungarischen Garde hätten, nicht zuletzt dank der enormen Aufmerksamkeit von Seiten der heimischen und ausländischen Medien, "das Bild Ungarns im Ausland erheblich geschädigt, insbesondere was das Vertrauen in die Stabilität und demokratische Reife betrifft".	In addition, the research institute believes that the extensive domestic and international media attention to Hungarian Guard actions has "significantly damaged Hungary's international image, particularly as regards belief in the stability of the country and in the sophistication of its democracy."	The Research Institute also believes that the activities of the Hungarian Guard, not least thanks to the enormous attention paid by the domestic and foreign media, 'have significantly damaged Hungary's image abroad, particularly as regards confidence in stability and democratic maturity'.
Wir erinnern uns: Seit Herbst 2006 ist die Reorganisation von radikalen und extrem rechten Gruppen in Ungarn kontinuierlich im Aufschwung, sodass seit Sommer 2007 mehrere, sich "nationale Selbstverteidigungsverein" nennende Organisationen gegründet wurden.	They point out that the increasing publicity and impetus given to the re-organization of radical and far right groups in Hungary starting in the autumn of 2006 have been part of the reason why a number of organizations calling themselves "national self-defence" alliances were established starting in the summer of 2007.	We remember that since autumn 2006, the reorganisation of radical and extreme right-wing groups in Hungary has been steadily on the increase, with the result that several 'national self-defence organisations' have been established since summer 2007.
"Diesen Gruppierungen ist gemein, dass sie sich jeweils als zivile Organisation definieren, während sie offen damit prahlen, ihre Mitglieder auf - mitunter bewaffnete - Verteidigungsaufgaben vorzubereiten (Katastrophenschutz, Landesverteidigung, Ordnungshütung), unter Berufung auf die Untauglichkeit der Polizei, der Armee, beziehungsweise des Staates selbst", hieß es.	"The common feature of these groups is that they call themselves civic organizations while openly declaring that they are preparing their members for defensive - including armed - tasks (citing disaster management, national defence, law enforcement) while declaring that the police and armed forces, in other words, the government, is unsuited for the role," Political Capital adds.	'What these groups have in common is that they define themselves as civil organisations, while openly boasting about preparing their members for defence tasks - sometimes armed - (civil protection, defence, law enforcement), invoking the ineffectiveness of the police, the army, or the state itself '.
Und weiter: Das alles geschehe gemäß jener Methode, die versucht, verschiedene, auf die Politik- und Parteiverdrossenheit der Bevölkerung basierende, politische Bestrebungen als bürgerliche Initiative zu tarnen.	They noted that all of these moves have been made within a configuration that relies on society's anti-politics and anti-political-party mood to cloak various political ambitions under a mantle of civic action.	And, furthermore, all this is in line with the method of trying to disguise various political aspirations based on the disenchantment of the people, which are political and party in nature.
Die Betonung des zivilen Charakters und die Vereinsform dienen also nicht bloß der Umgehung von juristischen Hürden, die im Zuge der Eintragung bei Gericht auftauchen könnten - es ist zugleich eine politische Strategie.	In other words, their emphasis on the civic nature of their actions and their choice of the association as their organizational form are not merely ruses to sidestep legal pitfalls to registration with the courts, but are also part of a political strategy.	The emphasis on the civil nature and form of association is not just a way of circumventing the legal obstacles that might arise from registration in court - it is also a political strategy.
Wie der Analyse zu entnehmen ist, stellen die Tätigkeiten der Ungarischen Garde einen risikoerhöhenden Faktor auch für die Beziehungen mit den Nachbarstaaten dar.	According to the analysis, the activity of the Hungarian Guard is heightening the risk of damaging our relations with our neighbours, too.	The analysis shows that the activities of the Hungarian Guard are a risky factor, including in relations with neighbouring countries.
"In den letzten Monaten wurde die Ungarische Garde in mehreren Nachbarstaaten als potenzielle Gefahrenquelle zitiert, so mancher ultranationalistischer Politiker bestimmter Nachbarländer sieht in der Entstehung der Ungarischen Garde die Bestätigung seiner eigenen Anti-Ungarn-Politik.	"In recent months several of Hungary's neighbours have cited the Hungarian Guard as a potential hazard. The ultranationalist political players among some of these neighbours have referred to the establishment of the Hungarian Guard as an argument to justify their own anti-Hungarian policies.	'In recent months, the Hungarian Guard has been cited as a potential source of danger in several neighbouring countries, while some ultranationalist politicians in certain neighbouring countries see the emergence of the Hungarian Guard as confirming its own anti-Hungarian policy.
Das alles hat Auswirkungen auf die politische Stabilität der Region" - hieß es.	All of these factors influence the political stability of the region," it adds.	All this has an impact on the political stability of the region '.
Aus der Sicht des Forschungsinstituts ist die Gründung der Ungarischen Garde kein Einzelphänomen in Zentral-Ost-Europa, somit ist das politische Risiko für die gesamte Region gewachsen.	The research institute notes that the establishment of the Hungarian Guard is not a unique phenomenon in Central and Eastern Europe, and as such it heightens the political risk for the whole of the region.	From the point of view of the research institute, the foundation of the Hungarian Guard is not a single phenomenon in Central and Eastern Europe, and the political risk for the entire region has increased.
Wie berichtet, sind die Tätigkeiten der Ungarischen Garde mit denen der Bulgarischen Nationalgarde vergleichbar, deren Gründung im August 2007 von der rechtsextremen Bulgarischen Nationalen Union (BNU) bekanntgegeben wurde. As reported, the activities of the Hungarian Guard are comparable to those of the Bulgarian National Guard, whose creation was announced in August 2007 by the extreme right-wing Bulgarian National Union (BNU).

Serious conflicts that broke out between Roma and non-Roma in a Sofia district (Krasna Polyana) were behind the establishment of the Bulgarian guard.	The emergence of the Bulgarian Guard has been the background to the mass Roma riots that have taken place in a district of Sofia (Krasna Poljana).

BNU took advantage of the disturbances to establish its guard, claiming that the goal of the organization was "national self-defence."	The BNU immediately took the events as an opportunity to establish the National Guard, arguing that the aim of organising 'national protection' was.

They argued that during the past 17 years Bulgaria had been subject to "Gypsy terror," in which the government was helpless and indifferent, Political Capital noted.	In fact, they believe that, over the last 17 years, a veritable 'Gypsy terror' has been seen in Bulgaria, but the state has remained inactive and indifferent - that is to say, political capital.
Und weiter: Die Initiative hätte eine heftige Debatte in der bulgarischen Öffentlichkeit losgetreten.	The initiative triggered heated debate among the Bulgarian public, it added.	Furthermore, the initiative would have sparked a heated debate in Bulgarian public opinion.
Wie gesagt, das erhöhte Risiko für ethnische Auseinandersetzungen wird auch durch die Tatsache belegt, dass einige bulgarische Roma-Organisationen angekündigt haben, zu Widerstandszwecken ihre eigene Garde zu gründen. Risk analysis reports would be published annually and, if risk-changing trends were to be identified, public opinion would be informed, as in the case of the risk assessment report.
Festtage sind nicht überall Feiertage	Holidays: Not everyone gets to enjoy the red-letter days	Forms are not all holiday days.
In Ungarn sind Feiertage gesetzlich genau geregelt, sodass sich die Praxis des Umdisponierens der Arbeitstage rund um die Feiertage mittlerweile etabliert hat, allerdings beschert uns das kommende Jahr weniger solche Tage.	Hungarian law names the red-letter days specifically, and reorganizing working days to increase the number of days off around the holidays has become a general practice, although next year we will not see quite so much reorganization.	In Hungary, public holidays are regulated by law, so the practice of rescheduling working days around the festive season has now become established, but next year brings us fewer such days.
Auch in der EU und in Amerika versteht man etwas anderes unter "Feiertag".	Holidays are not uniform in the EU or the USA either.	In the EU and America, too, we understand something different by 'festive day'.
Das ungarische Rechtssystem unterscheidet zwischen Staatsfeiertagen und arbeitsfreien Tagen.	The Hungarian legal system distinguishes among national holidays, state/bank holidays, and non-working days.	The Hungarian legal system distinguishes between state festivities and working days.
Arbeitsfreie Tage sind meistens kirchliche Feiertage, oder stehen mit bedeutenden historischen Ereignissen in Zusammenhang.	Non-working days are for the most part religious holidays and anniversaries of significant historical events.	Working days are mostly church holidays or are linked to important historical events.
Wir feiern zum Beispiel auch Neujahr: Sowohl der letzte Tag des alten, als auch der erste Tag des neuen Jahres sind arbeitsfreie Tage - Letzteres allein schon damit sich die Silvester-Feiernden ausruhen können.	Hungary celebrates New Year's Eve and Day: the final day of the old year and the first day of the new one are both non-working days - the latter if for no other reason, then to recover from New Year's Eve festivities.	For example, we are celebrating New Year: both the last day of the old year and the first day of the new year are free days - the latter alone, so that the New Year celebrations can rest.
Im ganzen Jahr haben wir insgesamt vierzehn Feiertage.	There are a total of eleven red-letter days in each calendar year.	We have a total of 14 public holidays all year round.
Die Staatsfeiertage sind der 15. März, der an die Revolution von 1848 erinnert, und der 23. Oktober, der Gedenktag der Revolution von 1956.	March 15 is a national holiday commemorating the revolution of 1848 while October 23 commemorates the revolution of 1956.	The State Day is 15 March, which is reminiscent of the 1848 revolution, and 23 October, which was the commemorative day of the 1956 revolution.
Am 20. August wird die Staatsgründung, am 1. Mai die Arbeit gefeiert, am 1. und 2. November gedenken wir unserer Toten.	August 20 marks the founding of the nation, while May Day is Labour Day. On November 1 and 2 we commemorate the dead, remembering our friends and relatives who have left us.	On 20 August, the founding of a state, the work of which will be celebrated on 1 May, will be commemorated on 1 and 2 November.
Darüber hinaus gibt es je zwei Feiertage zu Ostern, Pfingsten, und Weihnachten.	In addition, Easter, Pentecost, and Christmas are each two-day holidays.	Moreover, there are two days of celebration for Easter, Pfinest, and Christmas.
Da unsere Staats-, National- oder religiösen Feiertage selten auf ein Wochenende fallen, hat sich die Praxis der "Arbeitstags-Verschiebung" in den Fällen bewährt, in denen wir vor oder nach dem Feiertag nur einen Tag arbeiten würden.	Since our state, national or even religious holidays rarely fall on the weekend, it has become customary to reorganize the working week when there is only a single workday between the holiday and the weekend.	As our national, national or religious holidays rarely reach one weekend, the practice of 'working day postponement' has proved its worth in cases where we would only work one day before or after the day of the festive season.
Der Preis der verlängerten Wochenenden ist allerdings, dass wir an den Samstagen davor sehr wohl arbeiten, oder in die Schule gehen müssen.	The long weekend comes with a price however, which is to have to spend the preceding or succeeding Saturday at work or in school.	However, the price of extended weekends is that we do indeed have to work on the Saturday preceding that, or go to school.
Wann dieser Tag, der vor oder nach den Feiertag fällt, letztendlich abgearbeitet werden soll, wird seit langen Jahren vom Arbeitsminister in einer eigenen Verordnung festgelegt. Banken wollen Krise bewältigen	Banks Want to Solve Crisis	Banks want to overcome crisis
Die amerikanische Federal Reserve, die Europäische Zentralbank und die Zentralbanken Großbritanniens, der Schweiz und Kanadas haben beschlossen, gemeinsam gegen die Krise auf den Finanzmärkten zu kämpfen.	The American Federal Reserve Bank, The European Central Bank and the central banks of Great Britain, Switzerland and Canada have decided to fight against the crisis on financial markets together.	The US Federal Reserve, the European Central Bank and the central banks of Great Britain, Switzerland and Canada have decided to fight together against the crisis in the financial markets.
So werden mehr als 100 Milliarden Dollar vermittels Auktionen auf die Währungsmärkte gelangen.	More than $100 billion will enter the monetary markets by means of public sales.	More than USD 100 billion will be spent on the currency markets by auction.
Auf diesen Auktionen versteigern die Banken Zinssätze, zu denen sie bereit sind sich gegenseitig Geld zu leihen.	In public sales, banks bid on the interest rate for which they are willing to borrow money.	At these auctions, banks are selling each other up interest rates, and they are prepared to lend each other money.

It is the first time since the attacks of 11 September that the central banks of the various states have agreed on such a coordinated approach to avert or mitigate the consequences of a financial crisis.

Der Kongress stimmt der Richtlinie der MIFID zu, die am 1. November in Kraft trat.	Congress approves the transposition of Mifid that took place on November 1st	Congress agrees with the MIFID Directive, which came into force on 1 November.
Parallel zur parlamentarischen Ausarbeitung, die heute mit dem Kongressbeschluss im Senat über die dem Projekt zugehörigen Zusatz-/ Abänderungsanträge ihre Sitzung beendete, veröffentlichte die Regierung die Bestimmungen, die aus dem neuen Gesetz hervorgehen, mit der Absicht, das Inkrafttreten beider Regelungen bis zum Ende des Jahres zu ermöglichen.	Alongside its parliamentary proceedings, that ended today with the partial voting of the Congress on the amendments incorporated to the project in the Senate, the government has submitted to public hearing the regulation that will develop the new law, with the aim of coming in force before the year ends.	In parallel with the parliamentary process which has ended today with the Congressional Decision in the Senate on the supplementary amendments attached to the project, the government published the provisions arising from the new law with the aim of allowing both regulations to enter into force by the end of the year.
Die Vertreter der verschiedenen Unternehmen lobten einstimmig die Bemühungen der Kongress- und Senatsabgeordneten, die in ihren Verhandlungen und Abstimmungen das Ziel verfolgt hatten, die bestmögliche Regelung aufzustellen, die die Sicherheit der Investoren gewährleistet und die einzelnen Unternehmer-Aktivitäten reguliert, um so ein allgemein effizientes Marktgeschehen zu garantieren.	The representatives of different groups agreed in emphasizing the efforts made by deputies and senators to negotiate and agree the best legislation for guaranteeing the protection of the investors and regulating in detail the organizations activity so that the markets work efficiently.	The representatives of the various companies unanimously applauded the efforts of congressmen and senate members, who, in their negotiations and votes, sought to establish the best possible regulation, which would guarantee the safety of investors and regulate the various activities of employers, in order to guarantee a generally efficient market.
Die MIFID, die die Wertpapierdienstleistungsordnung neu festlegt, verfolgt zusätzlich zur Modernisierung der Finanzmärkte eine Verbesserung des Anlegerschutzes, die Erhöhung des Kontrollanspruches der spanischen Wertpapierkommission (CNMV) und die Förderung der Kooperation zwischen den verschiedenen Kontrollbehörden der Europäischen Union.	The Mifid, which amends the Securities Market Act, involves the modernization of financial markets, while it strengthens the investor protection, improving the supervisory powers of the Comisión Nacional del Mercado de Valores (CNMV) and encourages cooperation among the various supervisors of the European Union.	The MIFID, which redefines the investment services system, is pursuing, in addition to modernising the financial markets, an improvement in investor protection, an increase in the control requirement of the Spanish Securities Commission (CNMV) and the promotion of cooperation between the various supervisory authorities of the European Union.
Die neue Richtlinie ermöglicht es, sowohl spezialisierten Firmen als auch an natürlichen oder juristischen Personen Finanzberatungen anzubieten und trägt außerdem zur Errichtung neuer Finanzdienstleistungsunternehmen (ESIS) bei, den Beratungsunternehmen, die sich mit den Anlage- und Vermittlungsgesellschaften von Wertpapieren zusammenschließen.	The new regulations will grant financial advisory services to specialized companies as well as to natural or legal individuals, and creates a new type of financial advisory companies (ESIS), the financial advisory companies (AFI), that include stock firms, brokers, and the portfolio management firms.	The new directive will make it possible to offer financial advice to both specialised firms and to natural or legal persons and will also contribute to the creation of new financial services (ESIS), consultants, which will join forces with investment and intermediaries in securities.
Überdies erweitert sie die Anzahl der Systeme für die Ausführung von Finanztransaktionen, sodass den regulierten Umlaufmärkten die multilateralen Systeme des Effektengeschäfts und die Systeme zur Internationalisierung der Handelsaufträge hinzugefügt werden, welche schließlich mit den aktuellen Wirtschaftsakteuren in Wettbewerb treten würden.	In addition, it extends the number of systems available for the execution of financial operations, so included in the regulation are the secondary markets, the multilateral trading systems, and the internalization systems of orders, these will compete with the current stock market managers.	It also extends the number of systems for executing financial transactions so that the regulated circulation markets are supplemented by multilateral systems of transactions and systems for internationalising trade contracts, which would eventually compete with current economic operators.
Das Gesetz verpflichtet die Investment-Unternehmen, die Schwerpunkte ihres Unternehmensprofils, die Konfrontation und die Formen des Umgangs mit Risiken auf dem Markt kundzutun und alle durchgeführten Vorhaben zu registrieren, um so der CNMV ihre Kontrollaufgabe zu erleichtern.	The law also requires investment services companies to disclose to the market the key details of their business profile, risk exposure and forms of risk management, and to keep a registry of all their operations to facilitate the supervision by the CNMV.	The law requires investment firms to make known the priorities of their business profiling, the confrontation and ways of dealing with risks on the market and to register all projects carried out in order to facilitate the CNMV's supervisory role.
Die Wirtschaftskommission des Kongresses sah im Nachhinein noch weitere Änderungen vor, wobei der Beschluss, dass die mit Titeln versehene Schuldverschreibung nun aufgrund ihres hohen Risikogrades für den Investor als komplexe Finanzmittel gelten müssen, sich durch die US-Hypotheken- und Bankenkrise bestätigt hat. (US-Hypothekenkrise)	In their passage through the Committee on Economic Affairs of the Congress, several modifications were introduced, most notably securitised debts should be considered as a "complex" financial instrument due to its high risk for the investor, which has been demonstrated by what happened with the high risk American mortgages debts (subprime).	The Congress Economic Commission made further subsequent changes, with the decision that the titling of the debt must now be considered complex financial resources, given the high risk level for the investor, confirmed by the US mortgage and banking crisis.
Außerdem nutzte man das Inkrafttreten der Richtlinie zur legalen Eingrenzung der Arbeitsbereiche diplomierter Wirtschaftswissenschaftler; 30 Jahre nach dem 1977 die Verordnung, welche die für die Wirtschaftswissenschaftler reservierten Arbeitsbereiche einschränkte, erlassen wurde.	In addition, the transposition took advantage of the directive to legally define the functions that can develop graduates in Economics and Finance in 30 years after the decree approbation in 1977, that delimits the professional functions reserved to professional economists.	Furthermore, the entry into force of the directive on the legal limitation of the work of qualified economists was used; 30 years after 1977, the regulation was adopted restricting the areas reserved for economists.
Der Senat legte seinerseits neue Positionen im Finanzsektor fest, wie die des Wirtschaftsmediators, der auf fremde Rechnung arbeitet, keine Autorisierung seitens des CNMV benötigt und seine Dienste zur Kommerzialisierung von Produkten und zur Kundengewinnung gleichzeitig mehreren Investment-Unternehmen anbieten kann.	For its part, the Senate promoted the creation of new roles in the financial sector, such as the financial advisor, who will work for hire or reward, not require SEC approval and will be able to provide his services and marketing products brokerage to customers at various investment firms at the same time.	The Senate, for its part, established new positions in the financial sector, such as those of the economic mediator who works on foreign accounts, does not need authorisation from CNMV and can offer his services for the commercialisation of products and for after-sales, at the same time, several investment firms.

Die Versicherungsprämie ist der Preis einer Versicherung, der sich durch mehrere Faktoren zusammensetzt, u.a. Alter, Geschlecht, Zeitpunkt der Erstellung des Führerscheins, Familienstand, Art des zu versichernden Fahrzeugs oder dessen Nutzung. The insurance premium is the price of insurance which is made up of several factors, including age, sex, the time when the driving licence is being produced, the level of the family, the type of vehicle to be covered or the use of it.
Die Versicherungsunternehmen setzen ihre Preise entsprechend der Statistiken fest, sodass bei einer höheren Unfallgefahr auch höhere Beitragszahlungen fällig werden.	The insuring companies establish their prices based on the statistics, so that the greater the probability of having an accident is, the greater the premium is.	Insurance companies set their prices according to the statistics, so higher contributions are also required if the risk of accidents increases.

For this reason, both over 25 and women will have to pay less, because statistics show that, thanks to their caution, these groups have a lower accident rate.

After the Swedish newspaper 'Expressions' a few months ago raised doubts about the authenticity of Andy Warhols Brillo-Boxen in 1968, internal investigations in Moderna Museet in Stockholm are now reaching a sobering conclusion: the six 'Brillo-Boxes', which the former Museum Director Pontus Hultén has made available to Mona Museet in 1995, are copies - and perhaps the majority of the hundreds or so other 'Brillo-Boxes' of the type Stockholm 'that are circulating on the international art market.
Die Vorgeschichte ist verschachtelt, eine verwirrende Verkettung künstlerischer und kuratorischer Produktionen.	The history is convoluted, a confusing chain of artistic and curatorial productions.	The background is muddled, a confusing set of artistic and Kurdish productions.
